class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">邹幸彤、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赞查（藏）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">达日（藏）都是四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，二人皆因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">臧金达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西咸阳市法轮功学员。咸阳市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张鹏、王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏因为向淳化县民众发放真相资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月先后在各自的住所被淳化县公安局警察抓捕抄家。张鹏、王钰超（<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁左右）<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底在咸阳市住处被警察绑架，电脑、打印机等设备被抢走。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位法轮功学员被关押在咸阳淳化县看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均已被判刑，其中张鹏判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏约为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年不等，刑期不详。。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html"><span style="color: windowtext;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html</span></a><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">臧鸿燕：吉林</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">长春市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。臧鸿燕<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出现脑梗症状，被送往长春市中心医院病监大队，不准家属探望。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被朝阳区法院庭审，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日臧鸿燕被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/24/459153.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/24/459153.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">臧中美：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生。吉林省白城法轮功学员。臧中美原是吉林省梨树农场一名小学女教师，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年末因去北京上访被劳教一年半，释放回家后，丈夫和幼小的孩子因经受不住长期的警察上门骚扰被迫离婚。因她不放弃信仰，也被学校开除，流离失所到白城市打工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，臧中美骑电瓶车宣讲法轮功被白城市洮北区国保大队抓捕，并在其住处抄走大法书籍、电脑、真相资料、现金等物品。后被批捕。曾正在看守所绝食反迫害。臧中美<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现关押在长春女子监狱十三大队。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">泽让旦真（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州人，又叫“洛桑丹增”，阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因帮助同寺僧人彭措（又叫平措，已于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日自焚死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁）以自焚方式（指一种藏人抗议暴政、伸张正义的方式，即藏人自焚者把自己整个奉献出来，以清晰的理智、自愿的心态和惨烈的方式向暴政表达最强烈抗议的无奈选择，以期使公众舆论对极权和高压统治者予以最强烈的谴责或改变对手的情感），纪念中共当局镇压拉萨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件三周年，并在阿坝县城洽唐中街实施自焚行动；由于当地僧人和藏人为此举行了大规模情愿示威活动，随与中共军警发生冲突；其随后即被拉萨市警方抓捕、刑拘，并被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康县警方以涉嫌“购买汽油策划，鼓动、帮助自焚罪”执行逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案在四川省马尔康县法院开庭受审，最终被该法院更换罪名，以“故意杀人罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曾东平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，江西九江法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年出生，九江德安县某学校教师，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被逮捕，于同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日江西省九江市永修县法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年罚金一万，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日二审由九江中级法院，维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.yuanming.net/articles/a160640-%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.yuanming.net/articles/a160640-%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曾繁杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省梅州市梅县区法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">. 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时左右，曾繁杰在租住处遭梅州市公安局梅江分局金山派出所警察等抓捕，后被劫持到梅县区（扶大）看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日遭庭审，仅<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分钟便草草收场。后悉，曾繁杰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年并勒索<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元罚金。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曾凡锦：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，山东省菏泽市人，山东省郓城县育才路东段<span lang="EN-US">123</span>号公民，山东省郓城县公安局原经侦大队指导员，实名举报人，蒙冤警察。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2009</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，曾因和<span lang="EN-US">35</span>名警察联名向上级有关部门实名举报时任山东省郓城县县委书记刘国生严重贪污腐败，滥用职权操控黑白两道，强拆强占农民土地及打死打伤、肆意拘留农民等问题，并将此事发于网上，随遭被举报贪官刘国生等人严厉打压与疯狂报复；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其被不明身份数十人突然夜闯家中非法抄家和绑架，并送菏泽市东郊一处郓城县检察院私设审讯点关押，三天后被莫名刑拘；关押期间，该检察院副院长亲自带队，为让其在已捏造好的莫须有罪名签字认罪，采取连续<span lang="EN-US">50</span>天“车轮战”式审讯、长时间坐老虎凳和不给吃喝等多种酷刑对其折磨，甚至不惜另抓<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名与其关系不错的同事警察，以威逼利诱，酷刑折磨、逼疯逼残等方式强逼他们指控和捏造其犯罪事实；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其被转正式逮捕，后被菏泽市郓城县法院被以“贪污罪”枉法冤判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；后因其不服上诉，经菏泽市中级法院二审裁决，减为<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日获释后，其继续实名举报，并就刘国生、郑建生等官员的贪腐问题和其在狱中曾遭长期刑讯逼供，导致生命几经濒危等事实依法提起申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，刘国生因贪腐落马锒铛入狱，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日终被山东省泰安市中级法院以“受贿罪”从轻判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年；然而其早先为举报贪官而提起的申诉控告，却因山东当局官官相护，始终毫无结果；为求公道正义，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其遂网上发布《抬棺决斗宣言》，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月抬棺向山东司法机关发起生死决斗和法理辩论；此举一出，立时引来社会热议，但也旋即引起山东当局的极度不悦与强力打击；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，再度被当地警方抓捕，后被移交至山东省巨野县看守所刑拘；一个月后，被巨野县检察院以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，被山东省菏泽市巨野县法院以同罪名一审枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年；二审维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前疑在山东省菏泽监狱（山东省菏泽市定陶路<span lang="EN-US">61</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">274030</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曾加庚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1942</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁，住广州市海珠区。他毕业于华南理工大学材料科学与工程学院高分子材料专业，原广州珠江轮胎有限公司高级工程师。退休前，他是单位的技术骨干。因为讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾加庚被公交分局侦查二大队警察跟踪抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，他被广州市检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底，他被劫入广东省四会监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/21/446562.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾琴玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，湖南省郴州市柿竹园法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，郴州市北湖区政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”等部门多人闯到曾琴玲家抄家，抄走许多大法书和资料、电脑和多台手机等等。曾琴玲一直被关到郴州下眉桥洗脑，后被关押到郴州市梯子岭看守所。曾琴玲的丈夫怕受牵连早已与她离婚，一个女儿远在浙江杭州。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月曾琴玲遭郴州市苏仙区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/5/442112.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月生，女，家住鹤山市鹤城镇新联管区。曾尉英因修炼法轮功、并向大众宣传法轮功是教人向善，随被人恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾尉英被当地警方带走关押，其家被查抄。之后不久，其案很被构陷到检察院和江门市蓬江区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾尉英广东省江门市蓬江区法院被以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。现在广东省女子监狱二监区服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/2/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E7%9C%81%E9%B9%A4%E5%B1%B1%E5%B8%82%E6%9B%BE%E5%B0%89%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-430343.html"><b 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚饭后，曾小莉在家中被抓捕、抄家，被抢走大法书籍多本，还有法轮大法师父法像和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>些真相资料及<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘等私人物品。她被关押在梅州市蕉岭县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾小莉被逮捕，后被梅县区法院判处<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年刑期，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">50000</span>元。曾小莉不服提起上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，梅州市中级法院却枉法裁定维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/5/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E8%95%89%E5%B2%AD%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9B%BE%E5%B0%8F%E8%8E%89%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-430441.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/5/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E8%95%89%E5%B2%AD%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9B%BE%E5%B0%8F%E8%8E%89%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-430441.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曾兴阳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省广州市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月出生，广东省兴宁市人，大学毕业，原广东省茶叶进出口公司员工。曾兴阳、妻子邓芳、妹妹曾跃玲，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被天河区公安分局国保和石牌派出所警察抓捕，关押到天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，海珠区法院对<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人判刑，曾兴阳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；邓芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元；曾跃玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元。曾兴阳刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/11/447538.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/11/447538.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曾跃玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省广州市法轮功学员。曾兴阳的妹妹，<span lang="EN-US">1979</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出生，湛江师范学院毕业，在培训机构任职。曾兴阳、妻子邓芳、妹妹曾跃玲，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被天河区公安分局国保和石牌派出所警察抓捕，关押到天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，海珠区法院对<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人判刑，曾兴阳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；邓芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元；曾跃玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元。曾跃玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/11/447538.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/11/447538.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾又梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省聊城市东昌府区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被抓捕抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月庭审。曾又梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾志远：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省邵东市（原邵东县）水东江镇牛山村法轮功学员。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，曾志远多次被中共抓捕，三次被劳教，两次被判刑，在看守所、劳教所、监狱共被关押迫害十多年。曾志远<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被邵东市国保大队警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被邵东市法院判刑五年，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬被关押到娄底监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西达杰（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，炉霍寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。因中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，引发多地藏民强烈不满，四川省甘孜州炉霍县藏民随于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日（即当年中国农历新年初一）举行大规模和平示威活动；该活动随即遭到中共警方严厉的武力镇压和任意抓捕，致使多人被打死打伤及上百人被抓；至<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，已有<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人被中共当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月直至无期徒刑不等的刑期，另有数人被捕后完全失踪；扎西达杰亦因积极参与和平示威游行，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被警方以“参与和带头示威活动”为由从当地炉霍寺抓走刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以“炉火示威活动的主要带头人”判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。此前被羁押于四川省甘孜藏族自治州康定县监狱；目前在何监狱服刑，情况不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西顿珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县唐克镇人。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因独自在四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县城，身披佛教旗帜、手举大幅达赖喇嘛画像，以小跑方式在主要大道上开展抗议中共暴政的示威活动，随被当地警方在极短时间内控制、拘捕；据悉，此前其所在村镇藏民多年来一直因土地遭政府强占、暴力逼迁且得不到任何安置，而多次展开过和平请愿活动（含派代表进省城上访、集体静坐、呈交联署信、集会讨公道等），要求政府当局核实土地征用过程是否非法，并予以公正处理，但却无果而终；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，其被阿坝藏族羌族自治州地方当局正式逮捕，并被判处有期徒刑，罪名、刑期不详，服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西杰（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县人。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因拍录阿坝藏族羌族自治州藏人扎西顿珠身披佛教旗帜、手举大幅达赖喇嘛画像，在若尔盖县城大街上进行抗议中共暴政的抗议过程，并传于网上，随被当地警方于<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日左右抓捕、刑拘，具体罪由不详；据悉，此前其所在乡镇藏民长期因土地问题而被政府强占、暴力逼迁，得不到安置等所困扰，村民多次展开和平请愿活动而无果；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，其与扎西顿珠一起被阿坝藏族羌族自治州地方当局正式逮捕，并被判处有期徒刑，罪名、刑期不详，服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">帖林峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省南阳市<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁的法轮功学员，其妻子何喜梅退休前曾在南阳市沼气（现郑燃南阳燃气）公司任营业所长，一九九七年开始修炼法轮大法，在工作中，何喜梅兢兢业业干好本职工作，多次被单位、建委、省建设厅评为：“先进科室”、“建委十佳职工”、“省建设厅职业道德先进个人”等荣誉。她丈夫帖林峰也修炼法轮大法。一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，何喜梅和帖林峰曾多次遭中共迫害。何喜梅和丈夫帖林峰夫妻两人<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日都被南阳市公安局抓捕，关押在南阳市看守所。后获悉，何喜梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金三万元；帖林峰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金一万元。何喜梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。帖林峰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">展中香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，山东平度市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日与好友周玉香和周君一起到平度仁兆赶集，被仁兆派出所警察抓捕。后，展中香和周玉香分别被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，周君被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张爱民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市南票新区打渔山法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早上南票新区季屯派出所闯入张爱民家，没有出示搜查证，就抄家，并抓捕了张爱民、董艳红夫妇；张爱民于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被连山区法院被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金五千元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/15/457754.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/15/457754.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张保忠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北邢台市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年左右生，原为邢台农行第三营业部职工，一九九六年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月张保忠遭抓捕，先是被判缓一年六个月，而后被改为实刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期到：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。这是张保忠第二次遭受冤狱，他曾经被判刑七年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/14/458790.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/14/458790.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张朝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省潍坊市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午，张朝被当地警方抓捕到看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，张朝被潍坊市奎文区检察院批捕，所谓罪名是：以危险方法危害公共安全罪和妨害公务罪。据说，因此次事件国保谷志勇和奎文公安局长曹俊勇还被予以立功行为。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分，山东省潍坊市法轮功学员张朝，在潍坊市奎文区法院，第三次被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张成果：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年出生，河南省南阳市邓州人，大学毕业后在北京市打工。法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月发真相资料救人，六月三日被北京市昌平区回龙观派出所警察武钢等数人从家中抓捕，警察闯入张成果家中，将他双手反铐，抄走一台打印机、两台苹果电脑和手机以及大法真相资料等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被北京市昌平区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，上诉被驳回。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/4/2022-6-4.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/4/2022-6-4.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春蕾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西忻州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，张春蕾因要求各级政府公开关于迫害法轮功的政策而被非法抓捕。后被批捕，起诉。罪名是利用邪教破坏法律实施罪。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午忻州市忻府区法院开庭审理张春蕾利用邪教破坏法律实施案，文东海律师作为辩护律师参与开庭审理，该案检察院不让辩护律师阅卷，不接收辩护律师手续，不听取辩护律师意见。到了法院仍然不允许阅卷，不公开审理，没有庭审录音录像，在庭上只有法官检察官可以看卷，辩护律师和被告人均不让看卷，辩护律师拒绝就检察官口头念的证据目录发表质证意见，申请回避驳回，要求复议法官认为没有复议权利。后遭判刑，刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张春雷</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：贵阳仁爱归正教会长老。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，贵阳仁爱归正教会信众和几位外地来的基督徒在教会租的温州大酒店商住楼<span lang="EN-US">1702</span>房祷告，遭警方冲击，三位本地基督徒陈建国、李金芝和李林，以及从贵阳周边过来参加学习的基督徒共十人被带到延安中路派出所。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点左右，仁爱归正教会的张春雷长老赶到派出所交涉。在与派出所工作人员交涉过程中，张春雷长老被警察粗暴地推到在地，并遭扣押。后张春雷长老先是被口头通知行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天，但到期后未被释放。家属被口头告知张春雷长老已被刑事拘留但没有收到任何法律手续，主动询问办案单位和派出所，告知法律手续已寄出。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">中午，张春雷的妻子杨爱清师母去往派出所，拿到了贵阳市公安局云岩分局针对张春雷长老的逮捕通知书。据通知书所述，经贵阳市云岩区检察院批准，张春雷长老于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日<span lang="EN-US">15</span>时被以涉嫌诈骗罪的名义执行逮捕，羁押在云岩分局看守所。后转入贵阳市第二看守所。继<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日到<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日律师连续四天会见因遭遇到提审未见到以后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师会见张春雷长老再次受阻。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午九点，律师持会见手续到贵阳市第二看守所要求会见此前因被控“诈骗罪”而被羁押张春雷长老。接待民警称不能会见，理由是贵阳市国安局<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日向看守所发函，告知张春雷因涉嫌危害国家安全，在侦查期间未得到办案单位允许的情况下，禁止律师会见。律师要求对该文件复印或者拍照，被看守所民警拒绝。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底，张春雷案件从市检察院移交到市中级法院，至今为止已有四月有余，张春雷和律师都没有收到立案起诉意见书。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日上午，律师到贵阳中级人民法院阅卷，法院早已收到贵阳市检察院起诉书，以“涉嫌诈骗”和“煽动颠覆国家政权”起诉张春雷长老。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，律师在看守所会见了张春雷长老，春雷长老身体健康，精神也很好，平安喜乐。春雷长老也收到起诉书，明确表达了：信仰无罪，这些莫须有的罪名完全是对宗教自由的打压。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_69.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_69.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_75.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_75.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张春河：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月出生，广东省广州市人，广州市增城区荔城街公民，中级会计师，原广州市增城物协公司财务科长兼会计，原增城胶袋厂任聘员工，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早在<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年，即开始锻炼和信仰法轮功，并因个性大为改观，待人接物为人谦和，处处为他人着想，而在亲朋好友及单位里的同事中间称为公认的好人；但自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共开始迫害法轮功之后，其因一直坚持自由信念而成为广州市增城区“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”办公室的重点监控、打压的对象；曾被当局指派人员多次骚扰，并被<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次非法绑架、拘押；曾被强行关进戒毒所接受洗脑教育长达半年；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾被广州市增城区警方抓走并被迅速以邪教罪由处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，后被送到广州市槎头劳教所关押，同期，其被单位降两级工资；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，曾因北京奥运会即将召开，其在上班途中被增城区“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”办公室指使的增城警方和西园派出所便衣警察共同拦截，先后被关押在广州法制学校和增城区看守所，直至次年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被增城区法院冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，后在广东省女子监狱服刑；狱中，曾屡遭酷刑虐待，不仅被上手铐脚镣、被剥夺正常睡眠<span lang="EN-US">150</span>天，还被关小黑屋遭惩罚迫害若干天，导致其不能吃喝、大小便，造成肾水肿，出现生命垂危，最终狱方不得不将其送进广州武警医院救治；后其丈夫实在不堪压力重负而与其离婚，从此其被迫流离失所；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因其坚决抵制中共在“清零”行动中的强制洗脑转化，故而再遭广州市增城区警方和西园派出所警方联合抓捕，当日即被以涉嫌“邪教罪”刑拘，其家遭查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被增城区检察院以涉嫌同罪名正式批捕，并被关押在增城区看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案又被转到海珠区检察院，并被海珠区检察院以同罪由提起公诉；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其案在广州市海珠区法院庭审，终被一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；至今，尚不知其是否已提起上诉；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前被羁押于广州市增城区看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/4.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/4.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张春秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">益阳法轮功学员，男 ，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，张春秋与退休老教授高德思在湖南财专校园内被抓捕，张春秋被拘禁在益阳市第一看守所，惨遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后被开庭，最后与高德思被分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年与<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。狱中多次惨遭酷刑，直到“生不如死”。原本<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日服刑到期，但仍不予释放，直到<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日才准予出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，又被益阳市警方抓捕、抄家，并被关押在南县看守所，后被当局处劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，直至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，当其在街上行走时又被湖南省娄底市娄星区警方以涉“邪教罪”抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其案在娄底市娄星区法院庭审，当天被以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月。张不服，上诉中院，但<span lang="EN-US">2</span>审仍然维持原判。近日获悉，张春秋已在湖南省网岭监狱十监区服刑。因监狱方至今未通知家属刻意前往探监，且监狱方躲闪拒透其任何信息，故其狱中情况概不知晓。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://library.minghui.org/victim/i21870.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://library.minghui.org/victim/i21870.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张春耀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江省宁波市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日早上，张春耀被鄞州区中河派出所警察和鄞州区公安分局的国保抓捕并抄家，被关押到宁波市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被宁波市鄞州市法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/5/448542.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/5/448542.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省河源市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年出生，女，家住广东省河源市。她<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年底开始修炼法轮功，因向民众讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，她多次被拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午，张春英在向民众讲述真相时，遭人恶告，被河源市公安局警察抓捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日她被逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，目前被关押在广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/9/447439.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">张翠娟<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">广州市花都区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年出生，家住广州市花都区商业大道；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被广州市公安局花都区分局警察抓捕，关押到花都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被荔湾区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/27/2022-1-27.html#zip6"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/27/2022-1-27.html#zip6</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张德武：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">民营企业家、湖北襄大集团董事长。襄大集团是湖北省知名民营企业，上世纪<span lang="EN-US">90</span>年代，张德武从送鸡苗起步，白手起家创业，目前集团主营业务为农业畜牧养殖，并涉及化工以及房地产开发等，拥有襄大农牧、新鄂西化工、襄大建筑、襄大物流等生产经营板块，资产<span lang="EN-US">76</span>亿元人民币，员工<span lang="EN-US">7,100</span>余人。襄大集团曾在当地政府动员下，斥资七亿、承债式收购一个濒临破产的国企改制化工厂。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，因为张德武和债权人协商未果，债权人将化工厂告上法庭，襄阳中级法院便冻结了企业的基本账户。化工厂职工养老金停发、社保停缴，职工医疗费用无法报销。随后，将近八百名鄂西化工厂职工集体有序来到襄阳中院门口，聚集上访。此事被指为涉嫌“聚众冲击国家机关”，成为<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年张德武涉黑案的导火索。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，张德武及公司多名负责人被以涉嫌“聚众冲击国家机关罪”带走，继而被以涉黑移送审查起诉。一年后，张德武在<span lang="EN-US">17</span>年前，即<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年已审结无罪的一桩旧案，又被检察院重新提起抗诉。张德武被捕后，当地养殖户、村民、供应商纷纷站出来为其请愿，联名上书。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，湖北襄大集团董事长张德武被湖北省竹溪县法院一审认定犯寻衅滋事罪、非法拘禁罪、串通投标罪、高利转贷罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪，被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6013</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/13.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/13.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张迪</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张凤兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，女、哈尔滨市宾县宾州镇第二小学退休教师，<span lang="EN-US">998</span>年十<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共邪党开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，张凤兰被中共邪党抓捕、关押，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，张凤兰在讲述法轮功真相时，遭不明真相的人构陷，被哈尔滨市宾县公安局警察抓捕、抄家。当天，张凤兰被哈尔滨市宾县公安局国保警察关押到哈尔滨市第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，她被哈尔滨市依兰县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市尚志市法轮功学员。女。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日上午，她被尚志市公安局国保抓捕，并被刑事拘留，之后她被关押在哈尔滨拘留所。张凤莲<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张凤明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江绥化市法轮功学员。黑龙江省绥化市北林区<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日同时被绥化市北林区“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”及派出所警察抓捕，其中包括张连庆及妻子刘桂英、儿子张凤明，他们当天被关押到绥化市看守所。张连庆被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，目前关押在呼兰监狱；妻子刘桂英判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被关押到哈尔滨女子监狱；儿子张凤明判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被关押在北安监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a 0pt;">张国生：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">内蒙古赤峰市敖汉旗法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。早年修炼法轮功。在中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月发动迫害法轮功的运动后，张国生、卢连利夫妇因坚持修炼法轮功，经常遭当地“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”警察骚扰、搜查、抄家。张国生于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被警察抓捕，后被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。张国生的妻子卢连利身心受到极大打击，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日悲愤离世，终年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁。张国生被关押在敖汉旗看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/9/456601.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:
