lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张荣秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北辰区<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">法轮功学员。</span>张荣秀在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月份，因往树上挂法轮功挂件，被西于庄派出所抓捕，后“取保候审”回到家中。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月在这次清零中，先是西堤头大队找她谈话，让她在“三书”签字，被她拒绝后，西堤头大队将她的住房强行收回。当局又将挂法轮功资料事件重新审理，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，在网上开庭，张荣秀被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年刑期。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张荣秀被关押到李七庄女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/6/448766.html#2295221153-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/6/448766.html#2295221153-1</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张瑞君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东淄博市法轮功学员。五十多岁，新华书店退休职工，家住淄博市高新区四宝山镇。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年三月十九日左右，张瑞君被淄博市桓台县国保跨区抓捕，被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，桓台县国保对她拘留、查体，并批捕。警察强迫家人给张瑞君办健康码后，在体检不合格的情况下，将她关押在淄博市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张瑞君被二次开庭，是视频开庭。在视频中，家人看到她已被迫害得非常严重。原本身体健康的她，说话时，反应迟钝，精神萎靡不振，走路都成问题。她的孩子了解到张瑞君睡眠、吃饭都相当差。由于体检有传染病，她被单独关押在一间屋里，不与任何人接触、说话。第二次开庭后，张瑞君被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。她不服判决，继续上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，家属得知，她已被送入济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/14/%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E5%BC%A0%E7%91%9E%E5%90%9B%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E5%85%A5%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E5%A5%B3%E5%AD%90%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1-440043.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/14/%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E5%BC%A0%E7%91%9E%E5%90%9B%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E5%85%A5%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E5%A5%B3%E5%AD%90%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1-440043.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张少杰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，河南省南乐县人，前河南省南乐县基督教三自爱国运动委员会主席、基督教协会会长，第九届南乐县政协委员，南乐县基督教会牧师，中国在押良心犯。长期以来，因其身为牧师，经常帮助弱势群体维权解难，尤其是当信徒的合法权益受到侵害时，均想法给予及时的帮助与维权，随在当地备受信徒的喜爱，但这种行为却与政府某些人的利益发生冲突，随遭到当局的强烈不满和忌恨；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被南乐县警方在无任何法律手续的前提下强行从教会带走，其两个胞妹在众人的陪同下前去公安局要人，也被警察强行带走，其余人等亦遭警方堵截和殴打，之后才得知张少杰已被当地警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，又被追加涉嫌“妨害公务罪”予以批捕，但在起诉书中又显示将“妨害公务罪”变更为“诈骗罪”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，终被河南省南乐县法院以“诈骗罪”和“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。此前曾先后被羁押在河南省南乐县看守所和濮阳市看守所；目前在河南省新乡市河南第二监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张盛全：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。重庆市高新区石桥铺人。他原在石桥铺交易城做生意，公平交易，童叟无欺。张盛全曾屡遭中共迫害，他曾被非法劳教两年，在西山坪劳教所遭受过多种酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日重庆<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功学员张盛全、李嘉惠、李玉华、高洪伟、秦雪美，被抓捕两年多，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉已经被判刑。张盛全、李嘉惠，被枉判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；李玉华<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元，监外执行；高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；秦雪美<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。张盛全刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张淑萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东聊城市东昌府区名法轮功学员。张淑萍、王芹<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被聊城市东昌府区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>、国保大队、柳园派出所警察等抄家。王芹被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月左右被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。张淑萍的电动小汽车被安装了监控定位装置，在修车时被发现。张淑萍于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月上旬在高速路口被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底左右被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。王芹、张淑萍一直被关押在市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底左右被转送济南女子监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/25/2021-9-25.html#zip1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/25/2021-9-25.html#zip1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张淑琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江伊春市法轮功学员，女，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">，家住伊春市伊春区，在伊春经营一家旅店。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日当地警方对张淑琴经营的旅店进行搜查，并以「利用×教组织破坏法律实施罪」将张淑琴刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，将张淑琴批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日伊美区法院对张淑琴开庭审理。张淑琴本人没有到法庭现场，是在看守所以视频方式出庭。律师为张淑琴做了无罪辩护。张淑琴女儿刘春莉也为母亲做了无罪辩护。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张素英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏淮安市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，张素英<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日左右被淮安<span lang="EN-US">610</span>抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，张素英被清江浦区法院开庭， 一位维权律师出庭做无罪辩护。绑架、非法关押大半年，被淮安市清江浦区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。张素英老人已要求上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张树德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，哈尔滨市双城区新兴乡人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。自幼练习和笃信法轮功。哈尔滨工业大学毕业后，曾应聘于大连理工设计院，后外派到盘锦市高新技术产业开发区工作，是个诚实、可信、敬业的好青年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因居住证到期，张树德到所在地的兴隆台区兴盛派出所办理顺延手续时，当身份证录入相关信息时，警察问他有什么信仰，他称其信仰法轮功，随被拒绝办理居住证，并被威胁要对他调查。三天后，其居室遭搜查，本人被传唤做笔录。<span lang="EN-US"> 6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被双手戴着手铐非法送到盘锦市中心医院检查身体，然后就被强行刑拘于盘锦看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，他被盘锦市公安局兴隆台区分局正式逮捕，并将其案移交到兴隆台区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，检察院案将其案卷移交到兴隆台区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其案被盘锦市兴隆台区法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，张树德被该法院一审枉法重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。其不服上诉。其所在家乡的亲友得知其被冤判后，立刻决定伸出援手征签营救，同乡的父老乡亲们在极短的时间里，亲自填写上自己的名字或按下红手印，呼吁无罪释放张树德回家，目前已有<span lang="EN-US">1744</span>人签名声援。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张顺新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆喀什地区泽普县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁，在中共对法轮功持续至今近二十年的迫害中，他因修炼法轮功在<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，但他挺过来了。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚十点左右，张顺新被塔西南石油基地公安局（隶属于泽普县公安局）警察冯海洋骗到派出所后，再次被绑架关押抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，新疆喀什地区公安局警察到法轮功学员张顺新家通知亲属，张顺新现被关在农三师图木舒克市盖米里克监狱。亲属这才知道张顺新于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并在亲属、律师不在场的情况下秘密宣判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张堂江：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东平度</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，家住山东青岛平度市旧店（祝沟）镇祝沟前村。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，平度市政法委人员闯进张堂江家后，叫来祝沟镇派出所警察将他抓捕到祝沟镇派出所关押，并抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午，张堂江的律师给平度门村看守所打电话，看守所人员告知律师，张堂江已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/30/2022-5-30.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/30/2022-5-30.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张廷福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁老人张廷福在达州下火车，被达州车站派出所拦截扣押后刑事拘留，问其原因，是重庆上清寺派出所将张廷福上传为网上追逃人员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日重庆维权人士张廷福，被重庆市公安局渝中区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑拘，现羁押在渝中区看守所。家属经多方投诉后，才于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日拿到刑事拘留通知书，张廷福也从达州转至重庆渝中区看守所，得知成为逃犯的原因，是派出所以其涉嫌寻衅滋事罪，上传为网上追逃。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张廷祥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">贵州省安顺市平坝县新艺厂（<span lang="EN-US">170</span>厂）法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始迫害法轮功后，张廷祥坚持修炼，多次被迫害，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，张廷祥被贵州省贵安新区<span lang="EN-US">30</span>个警察入室抓捕、抄家，抢走电脑、书籍、手机等几箱子私人物品，还劫走了张廷祥个人现金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元。张廷祥被关押在平坝看守所，后被关押在安顺市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被贵阳市南明区法院判刑：张廷祥获刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">张伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，家住东港市。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，丹东市委、政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”与丹东市公安局秘密策划，经过长期电话监控以及各种监控手段、跟踪监视，对丹东市公安系统统一部署，丹东国保支队警察倾巢出动，加上直属公安分局以及法轮功学员所在地公安派出所为主力，合计至少一千几百人参与此次抓捕。此次行动，东港市<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员被抓捕。张伟也遭抓捕和抄家，抢走法轮书籍、资料若干、笔记本电脑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>台、打印机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台、几部手机。张伟被关进丹东看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，辽宁丹东地区东港市法院对<span lang="EN-US">11</span>名法轮功学员非法庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，东港市法院对法轮功学员下达判决。张伟被非法判重刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，现非法关押在辽宁女子监狱<span lang="EN-US">1</span>监区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>小队。张伟一直坚持炼功，曾多次被打骂、体罚、强制“转化”，张伟曾绝食反迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张维柱：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1958</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河南省籍人，天主教徒，教名<span lang="EN-US">Joseph ZhangWeizhu</span>，河南省新乡市天主教教区（下简称“新乡教区”）主教，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年获梵蒂冈任命成为主教以来，因在河南省新乡教区拥有约<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万名信众，且拒不加入中共设立的中国天主教爱国会（简称 “爱国会” ），故而其主教称位一直不被当局承认；曾因此而被当局多次抓捕、刑拘和软禁；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，曾因坚决维护信仰而被中共当局秘密软禁达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多之久；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日起，因中共开始实施新制“宗教教职人员管理办法”，规定宗教教职人员必须“拥护中国共产党领导”，故而其及诸多天主教神职人员，凡拒绝登记加入官方“爱国会”者均被成为率先监控、打压的对象；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因在河北省沙河桥一处工厂区设立修道院，以教牧培养神职人员，突遭河北当局百余名警力包围该修道院，后被以不明罪由抓捕，同天张维柱与另<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名神父，以及正在上课的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多位修士亦被抓捕，至自此失联；截至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其已被超期关押近一年之久，依然尚未释放，并且音信全无。目前被羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/blog-post_40.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/blog-post_40.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张文斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">原籍山东、原定今年大学毕业。因<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在微信实名公开发布“习近平下课”、“共产党下课”视频后，其微信被封杀，后又遭强迫失踪，目前处于失联状态。此前他曾因言获罪被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天。张文斌说，自己挺身而出，武汉肺炎疫情是导火索。而这段矛头指向习近平的视频使他又遭遇了强迫失踪。目前没有进一步的信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张文和：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，北京市通州区人，回族，<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁以前信仰伊斯兰教，<span lang="EN-US">51</span>岁以后皈依基督教，早年曾为北京花丝镶嵌厂、北京玉器厂职工，“张文和工艺品有限公司”创办人和经营者，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-1979</span>年时期“西单民主墙运动”（简称“民主墙运动”）参与者，政治异议人士，民主人权活动家，中国在押政治犯。早年曾经历文化大革命十年浩劫磨难，小学三年级及被迫辍学，自此被定性为资本家的狗崽子而备受凌弱和不公；<span lang="EN-US">1979</span>年，曾因参与“民主墙运动”而遭北京当局刑拘<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，且刑拘期间受尽酷刑折磨；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代，为谋生计和筹集款项，曾开办“张文和工艺品有限公司”，其工艺品因质量精美优秀幸得被海湾伊斯兰国家博物馆收藏；之后，又因其乐善好施，随曾多次为清真寺捐款，并变卖其在通州区的三间房屋，将所得款项全部捐助给回民孩子用于阿拉伯语的学习；此期间，因追求民主人权理念而积极参与维权活动，曾<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次被北京当局送进精神病医院，接受惨无人道的人权迫害；近年来，因其放胆言论，呼唤<span lang="EN-US">"</span>颜色革命<span lang="EN-US">"</span>、倡导<span lang="EN-US">"</span>三民主义<span lang="EN-US">"</span>和<span lang="EN-US">"</span>新兴中会<span lang="EN-US">"</span>，呼吁中共与民主力量以及联合国为政治改革举行三方会谈而备受当局注目和敌视；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因不堪遭受中共政府愈加疯狂的逼迫而被迫前往巴林王国避难，但同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因其签证过期被捕，并被关在当地警局，之后即被遣返回国；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其再被北京市通州区中仓派出所警方带走，当天即被关进精神病院，并不许家属探视；其妻王素娥为此立即成立“营救张文和”群组，呼吁社会正义人士对其丈予以高度关注，同时，剃发明志，誓言维权到底；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，终于知其被关具体地址，但警方拒透其一切具体细节，只称<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日要做司法鉴定，结果得出后或被移转其他地方；据悉，其曾自曝被拘押在北京市公安局看守所期间，曾惨遭警方酷刑虐待，被狱警按在地上，从背后戴上“紧铐”，并将其头套上防毒面具，后又被上“死铐”，昼夜戴“背铐”<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个多月，直至被刑拘关押看守所<span lang="EN-US">19</span>个月后，再被送到北京市延庆监狱中的精神病医院继续关押长达<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，且历次被关精神病院，历次被强迫大量吃药，导致其身心伤害极大。目前被羁押于北京市通州区精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">张文英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，贵州省黔东南苗族侗族自治州（简称黔东南州）凯里市人，侗族（需再核实），基督徒，黔东南州凯里市基督复临安息日教会神职人员，聚会点负责人及长老，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代初成立基督复临安息日教会聚会点以来，因一直作为教会长老热心服侍教会并照顾信徒的一切事工活动，随被众信徒广为喜爱及信任；但因其所属教会拒不认同也不接受中共当局认可的“三自教会”管理，属于地下家庭教会<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余年，虽早已向贵州省宗教局提交教会聚会点合法申请，但始终未获审批，故遭贵州当局在意识形态上的严苛管理；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又因其教会聚会点信徒不断增多，教会势力日渐强大，所以很快引起贵州省黔东南州当局关注与恐慌，并刻意成立项目组，对其聚会点进行全面侦查；之后，其被黔东南州凯里市警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘，自此失联，另有<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名教会神职人员亦被以“同案犯”抓捕刑拘；后其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均被黔东南州凯里市检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其因聚会点申请未被国家审批，众信徒所交奉献款均属于诈骗款，故而其行为属于违法；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案被当地凯里市法院一审以“诈骗罪”统一宣判，其因是教会长老而被枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月；另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位神职人员亦被枉判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>—<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年不等刑期；其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人不服判决，已向黔东南州中级法院提起上诉，二审正在等待中。目前被羁押于黔东南州凯里市看守所（贵州省<span lang="EN-US">/</span>黔东南苗族侗族自治州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>凯里市<span lang="EN-US">/</span>永乐路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">556099</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张喜维：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西省法轮功学员。陕西省礼泉县人。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被西安市雁塔区公安分局国保大队抓捕、关押构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被西安市雁塔法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/27/452405.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/27/452405.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张霞（大连）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁左右，大连市中山区人，原中山区青云小学教师，法轮功学员，良心犯。因信仰法轮功并起诉江泽民，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，被送洗脑班<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在学校上班时间又被大连市国保与民主广场派出所警方联合绑架抓走，家被查抄，电脑及相关法轮功资料等均被搜走。其丈夫孙俊区派出所问询，已被扣押，后得知夫妇二人均被关押在大连市姚家看守所羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其被大连中山区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年被大连市中山区法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，大连市中级法院未经二审即对她维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，张霞被送往辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张霞（张家口）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张霞、张秀玲、邢果花（现年<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁）三人都是张家口市张北县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下午三点多，张北县国保大队四个警察（便衣），以调查一些事为由，在张霞家楼下强制张霞戴手铐绑架；五点多以同样的手段绑架了法轮功学员邢果花；六点多又绑架了法轮功学员张秀玲。随后讲他们关押到张家口看守所关押；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被到张北县检察院；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被构陷到张北县法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被张北县法院秘密判刑，张霞<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款三万元；张秀玲<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款两万元，邢果花<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款两万元。张霞向张家口中级法院上诉。邢果花、张秀玲已经于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被转入到石家庄女子监狱迫害。张霞刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/25/444048.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：湖北武汉法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日因发法轮功资料被武汉市江岸分局行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，后被送往武汉市江汉区洗脑班迫害，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被武汉市公安局江岸区分局辞退，失去了工作。在洗脑班，她被限制人身自由，被逼洗脑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日晨，张霞在家中被破门而入的河南省洛阳市公安局涧西公安分局警察抓捕，并将她从武汉抓捕至洛阳。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，将张霞送至洛阳看守所。张霞于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被洛阳市公安局涧西分局逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，河南省洛阳市涧西区法院判张霞<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，剥夺政治权利年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，其冤判的所谓罪名是“利用通讯信息网络宣扬邪教，破坏国家法律、行政法规实施”。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a lang="EN-US">2</span>人又被东风派出所抓捕。隔离<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后，张宪军被关押在双城看守所，徐艳被关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所。之后一直没有<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人消息 。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日张晓东遭当地警方刑事拘留，后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被批准逮捕。其代理律师会见受到限制。目前警方还在侦查。张晓东现羁押在南昌市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_48.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_48.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_77.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张晓华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">昆明市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁，昆明市人，曾因修炼法轮功被判刑迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午，张晓华到官渡区子君路星云园小区朋友家串门，被警方抓捕，随后张晓华家被搜查。同时被抓捕的还有田云波、李萍等人。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日张晓华、李萍、田云波被五华区法院视频庭审，后被判刑：张晓华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，李萍<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，田云波<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。张晓华刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/18/%E6%98%86%E6%98%8E%E5%B8%82%E5%BC%A0%E6%99%93%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E6%9D%8E%E8%90%8D%E3%80%81%E7%94%B0%E4%BA%91%E6%B3%A2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-441414.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/18/%E6%98%86%E6%98%8E%E5%B8%82%E5%BC%A0%E6%99%93%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E6%9D%8E%E8%90%8D%E3%80%81%E7%94%B0%E4%BA%91%E6%B3%A2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-441414.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张小麦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原名陈煜，浙江临海市基督徒。张小麦</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈煜）因在开设网上书店“小麦书房”销售基督教书籍</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">,</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被捕</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">,</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在张小麦于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被中共当局以「网上销售非法境外宗教出版物」被捕后，公安部曾通报全国，要求各地国保根据从「小麦书房」搜到的发货订单接触收货人，就其购买书籍的取向和「当地非法宗教活动的情况」进行取证，有上万人被问询。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">27</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日一审判决，以非法经营罪判</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑。并处以罚金</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万，所扣押</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12864</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本书予以销毁。判决书同时裁定，被告除了被罚</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元外，还须追缴售书违法所得的</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元上缴国库，无法追缴的，由被告退赔，并须予判决生效后十天内缴纳。这是对传播基督教的基督徒的赤裸裸的镇压。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，二审维持原判。刑期至：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2026</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/7.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/7.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张小娜</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：辽宁省葫芦岛市绥中县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日生，家住葫芦岛市绥中县前所镇前所村。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，她开始修炼法轮功。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，绥中公安局国保大队抓捕了张小娜，并抄家，之后，她回家，被所谓“监视居住”。在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，张小娜又被带走。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。被关押在葫芦岛市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/20/447877.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/20/447877.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张小平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛阳维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号，洛阳政府为了修建西环路，在程序不合法的情况下，对张小平家宅基地上的房屋进行了强拆，张小平也因此被逼自学法律，走上了依法维权抗争之路。张小平通过信息公开、行政诉讼等法律途径获取了一些关于修建道路的政府信息，通过对这些信息的分析，发现了前洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身违法修建西环路造成至少<span lang="EN-US">1</span>亿元国有资产流失的事实。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，张小平就这一事实，实名向驻河南中央第一巡视组<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号邮寄了一封《举报信》，此信查询单显示<span lang="EN-US">3.28</span>日已经妥投。巡视组不但没有保护张小平举报人的身份，此举更是将张小平暴露在被举报人的眼皮之下，被打击报复也是迟早之事；因为举报的事情，张小平接到过威胁电话。关于泄漏举报人信息的问题，张小平通过新浪微博发声质疑，并要求相关部门查处。其最后一个博文发于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，结果，违法人员没得到查处，举报人却被抓了进去。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，洛阳公民张小平疑因举报厅级干部被刑事拘留，其丈夫张智斌行政拘留。原因疑是他们向中央巡视组举报原洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身（正厅级干部）。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张小平被洛阳公安局南昌路分局（电话<span lang="EN-US">0379-64316110</span>）抓捕；涉嫌罪名是“寻衅滋事”，<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日早被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被批捕。羁押在洛阳看守所。后无进一步信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张小琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆涪陵区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，女。张小琴<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在涪陵讲法轮功时被构陷，被涪陵区国保警察抓捕、抄家。抄走电脑、打印机、大法书籍等物品，后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张小琴被批捕。被绑架构陷大半年后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被重庆南川区法院庭审，后悉被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省郑州荥阳市法轮功学员，女，一九九七年和丈夫李秦军开始修炼法轮功。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1999</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共邪党开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，她和丈夫李秦军多次被抓捕、关押。张小荣被劳教期间被迫害致精神失常，她丈夫李秦军两次被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被荥阳市公安局国保与京城派出所恶警联合抓捕，关押在郑州第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><b lang="EN-US">8</span>年。据知情人透露，目前张秀兰身体已极度虚弱，浑身瘦得皮包着骨头，生命时刻处于危险之中。即使这样，她在看守所里还被逼转化、被逼在诬判书上签字，她不答应转化、签字，狱警就打她骂她。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，张英女士被开庭。后获知被常州市武进区法院判张英<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日获悉，辽宁省锦州市凌海市法院对这名老人下达判决，其中张英玲、金晓梅都被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；康桂云<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span
