宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">翟登蕊、李思琪、侯金艺、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、阿旺觉尼（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生年月不详，籍贯不详（只知藏区僧人），西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺密宗学院经师，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并长期在西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺密宗学院研习、进修；因曾长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成为其主要弟子之一，遂被哲蚌寺密宗学院立为经师（即精通佛教经藏的僧人，又称佛教讲经诵经的师父）；又由于其受教尊师兰林仁波切是深受藏民普遍敬重的哲蚌寺喇嘛，地位、声望及影响力并非由政府任命，因此被当局视为异己予以排挤、管控，其因与之交往甚密，故而亦成为当局长期监控打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因藏区发生以僧侣为主的大规模抗议示威活动，以期达到让中共当局真正实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并呼吁准许达赖喇嘛回国返乡等政治诉求，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其所在哲蚌寺<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧侣亦参与其中，致使抗议行动很快扩展至整个拉萨市区及四川、青海等藏区；针对此，西藏当局很快派遣大批持枪武警予以极端管控，双方发生严重对峙与冲突，随后即有众多僧侣被抓捕，其余人等被遣返寺庙严加看守；尽管此前其并未参与游行抗议，但是，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日其仍被拉萨市警方以涉嫌“参与抗议活动”抓捕，自此长期失联；另有二名哲蚌寺好友、学者僧侣亦被一同抓捕；后被拉萨市检察院转正式批捕，罪由竟是“未能阻止哲蚌寺僧人举行大规模抗议行动”；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在被长期羁押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，被拉萨市中级法院以不详罪名密判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，因长期失联，其狱中具体境况均无下落。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、高恒：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，湖北省黄冈市蕲春县漕河镇上河桥村人，广东省广州市番禺区南浦岛常驻居民，基督徒，广州圣经归正教会信徒，公益人士，中国在押良心犯。因其为人正直，热心公益，笃信基督，经常自觉参与所在教会的各种事工（即服务活动），故经常受到所在教会及区域的民众好评（如<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，因广州市再次出现新管病毒升级版疫情，其所在番禺区南浦岛处于封闭管理状态，随百姓生活出现诸多不便，其所在圣经归正教会为此开展了为市民发放生活物资等活动，其一直踊跃参与其中，即是一例）；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，曾因在儿童节当天举牌呼吁“尊重生命”、“反对堕胎”，而令当局不满，次日即被广州市番禺区南浦岛警方强行要求房东对其驱离，后因其及房东持守立场，顶住压力，终未妥协；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，“六四事件”第<span lang="EN-US">32</span>周年受难者纪念日，因其在广州地铁<span lang="EN-US">2</span>号线某地铁站举牌“六月四日，为国家祷告”，并将相关图片发于网上，同时在微博上写下：“一切社会层面上的苦难，虽然往往被归结于制度与政治的丑恶，然而，究其根本，它无不源于人心中根深蒂固的罪性。就这一罪性而言，我们与屠杀的决定者、指挥者和执行者，并无根本的不同。感谢主，我们虽同为罪人，却蒙了从上帝而来的奇异恩典，悔改认罪，接受耶稣为主，从而成为上帝的儿女”等心得，很快被广东网警发现告发，遂顿遭广州当局强力打击；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日凌晨，即被广州市番禺区南浦岛派出所警方从家中抓走，自此失联；据悉，其友人称应该已被广州市公安分局警方刑事拘留，涉嫌罪名寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被正式逮捕。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高恒因在六四<span lang="EN-US">32</span>周年（<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年）纪念日在广州地铁站举牌呼吁为国家祷告而被控寻衅滋事一案于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日终被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。目前仍关押在番禹看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/110-202344.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/110-202344.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_42.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_42.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、贡嘎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生年月不详，西藏自治区拉萨市林周县人，拉萨市林周县旁多乡藏民，职业不详，生态环境保护者，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早从<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年起，中国政府就开始计划将在拉萨市林周县附近的矿区建设、实施“旁多水利枢纽工程”。因该工程要在两条交汇于林周县旁多乡的河流——热振河、旁多措河之上筑坝截水，故为确保顺利开工，相关政府部门就于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年两次召开藏民大会，郑告村民此工程是“中共中央的指令，若有藏人试图阻止施工，将以政治罪名进行拘捕”。随后几年，因有关部门迅速投入大量施工准备，不仅在当地做频繁测量、建桥及建路等工作，而且炸山挖石，大量采矿，随意排放污水，导致当地的自然生态环境出现严重毁坏，附近村民的民房出现裂痕及大面积农田被毁坏等现象。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因拉萨市林周县的“旁多水利枢纽工程”正式开工，当局随立即强迫旁多乡<span lang="EN-US">119</span>户（近<span lang="EN-US">700</span>名）藏民尽快整体搬迁。因当地藏民不愿搬迁，故而多次向政府部门提出投诉请求，但均毫无果效。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，遂被迫进行集体维权与和平请愿，以期能借此阻拦破坏生态环境的采矿项目。不料却遭到中共西藏当局的强烈打压。贡嘎、白玛等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名藏族人权捍卫者因此遭拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，贡嘎、白玛等一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人案分别被拉萨市法院以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由秘判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等徒刑，其亦被判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前在西藏自治区第一监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">4</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、韩仕民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京延庆法轮功学员，杨进香的丈夫，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日生，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月十<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，韩仕民开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚，杨进香和丈夫韩仕民，以及郭金山、吴方玲等被抓捕。郭金山和韩仕民被关押在延庆看守所，杨进香和吴方玲被关押在昌平看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日家人得知，北京延庆区吴方玲、杨进香、韩仕民、郭金山被判刑——吴方玲<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，杨进香<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，韩仕民<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，郭金山<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。韩仕民刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/13/447593.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/13/447593.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、华丽琴<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东聊城市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚，济南市铁路公安局、聊城市火车站派出所联合聊城市东昌府区国保大队、古楼派出所共十几个警察，闯入聊城市东昌府区法轮功学员华丽琴家中，把陈军、华丽琴、孙秀娥、李桂华、张亮、徐绍霞（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）和华丽琴的丈夫共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人，抓捕到火车站派出所。火车站派出所对每位学员采指纹、勒索每人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元保证金，同时在当晚和第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天分别对<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位法轮功学员及郭秀萍等抄家，抢走了大法书、真相资料和个人财物。第二天后取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/31/2021-8-31.html#zip7"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/31/2021-8-31.html</span></b></a></span><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">6</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、贾蕊菱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西西安市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，长安区韦曲派出所警察抓捕了贾蕊菱，一直将她关押在西安看守所，长达<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年多。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，西安雁塔法院对贾蕊菱判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。又过了约<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，即<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，贾蕊菱被劫持到陕西省女子监狱。仅<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月就出现大小便失禁状态，狱方让家属送尿不湿。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/19/446444.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/19/446444.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、姜淑娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省莱西法轮功学员。原是山东省莱西市汽车站职工，她因坚持对法轮功的信仰被开除公职及遭受多种迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日姜淑娥在做家政的户主楼下遭莱西国保李为魁等人绑架，关押在普东看守所，后被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李大尧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省荆州市监利县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年六十六岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午十一点左右，监利县国保大队、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”、县公安局、特警出动大量警力，在同一时间合谋抓捕了李大尧、李乐成、朱春新、何成、王升贵五位法轮功学员，不由分说直接把人从家里带走，紧接着非法抄家，家中被翻得一片狼藉，电脑等大量私人物品被全部抢走，没留下什么清单。其中李大尧家的门被警察请来的撬锁人强行撬开。李大尧<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后上诉，荆州中级法院维持原判。李大尧<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被劫持到在湖北省范家台监狱关押。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）和华丽琴的丈夫共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人，抓捕到火车站派出所。火车站派出所对每位学员采指纹、勒索每人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元保证金，同时在当晚和第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天分别对<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位法轮功学员及郭秀萍等抄家，抢走了大法书、真相资料和个人财物。第二天后取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日上午被当地五洲派出所抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被梅州市梅县区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，罚款一万五千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span 12.0pt;">、孙永勤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，家住东港市。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点多钟，孙永勤在开车回家的路上，被便衣警察劫持，车和钥匙被抢。十点左右，妻子张小平正坐在客厅沙发上看书。十多个便衣警察拿着抢到的门钥匙破门而入，将张小平和她女儿铐住，当时张小平的女儿已经睡下，恶警在被窝里将她抓捕。恶警疯狂抄家，抢走法轮大法书籍、真相资料若干、现金十万余元（家中生活费及生意周转资金，还有她女儿的工资<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元均被洗劫一空）、手机、存折、银行卡、打印机<span lang="EN-US">3</span>台、电脑两台。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口全被恶警非法抓捕到东港市开发区公安所审讯。孙永勤、张小平被非法关押进东港看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，东港市法院对孙永勤重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，现被非法关押在沈阳第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>监狱<span lang="EN-US">2</span>监区<span lang="EN-US">2</span>小队。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 159.5pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">13</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、庹万学：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日庹万学被抓捕关押。此前，庹万学曾被判重刑，在德阳监狱遭酷刑迫害。后得知，庹万学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，已被关押到乐山嘉州监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在家中被派出所警察抓捕，两所住房被警察抄家，大法书籍、真相资料、电脑、现金（约<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>元一元真相币，还有金额不清的美元）等被警察抢走。据悉王敬琳在成都机投镇某小区发真相资料被构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被开庭，当庭未宣，于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span minor-fareast;">15</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、王淑敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，王淑敏被天津宁河公安分局、宁河芦台镇派出所、街道，联合抓捕，一直被非法关押在宁河区看守所，期间两次抄家。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">16</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、夏月仙</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：武汉市江汉区法轮功学员。年过七旬。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日是中秋节，其带着孙子玩耍，顺便善意地告知民众法轮大法好的真相，遭警察抓捕，被关押到东西湖第一看守所。一年多后，即<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">17</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、严精华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江西省南昌市法轮功学员，女，一九六一年生，她因坚持修炼法轮功、宣传法轮功，多次被中共当局抓捕、关押，三次被判刑，累计遭冤刑十二年半，三次她都被关押在江西省女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月抓捕后遭中共判刑判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。她的儿子也因中共的株连迫害政策失去了理想的工作。严精华刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/22/457033.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/22/457033.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">18</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、尹君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省白山市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生，吉林省白山市抚松县人。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年年底，当时<span lang="EN-US">17</span>岁的尹君开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，正读高三的尹君面临高考，被迫辍学；她曾多次被抓捕、关押，两次被劳教、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑。尹君<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被抓捕，关押在长春市第四看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，她两次被长春市朝阳区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，尹君被长春市朝阳区法院<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月</span>。她已提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日又被转到吉林省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/28/446906.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/28/446906.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">19</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、赵淑芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年出生，内蒙古自治区呼伦贝尔市莫力达瓦达斡尔族自治旗（莫旗）人，满族，呼伦贝尔市莫旗中心商店下岗职工，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月起，因笃信和宣传法轮功，曾屡遭内蒙古自治区自扎兰屯市“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”管理办公室、国保大队警方及公检法司法部门等的监控、打压和逼迫；曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被劳教，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被拘押，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被强送洗脑班受迫害，以致其夫离女散，被迫流离失所，长期有家不能回；狱中曾遭到野蛮灌食、串“糖葫芦”、戴支棍儿脚镣、灌盐水、上大挂、奴工等虐待；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其及法轮功好友任小梅一同准备搭乘往返扎兰屯市往返莫旗的大客车时，突遭莫旗客运站乘警拦截，在拒绝其手机被扫码、身份证被检查之后，很快二人被赶来的当地警方非法抓走，后被刑拘于内蒙古阿荣旗看守所；之后，被扎兰屯市检察院以涉嫌邪教罪转正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其二人案在扎兰屯市法院被以网络视频方式开庭受审；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其被该法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日；</b>同案任小梅亦被该法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日已刑满释放。赵淑芝目前在内蒙古自治区第一女子监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3_7.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3_7.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">20</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、郑大海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁大连中山区法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月出生，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在家中被抓捕，遭抄家，羁押于大连姚家看守所，后被视频开庭。近日获悉，郑大海被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-439997.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">21</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、曹芷馨：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年出生，中国人民大学历史系硕士毕业生，北京大学出版社编辑，北京白纸运动抗议者，中国在押政治犯。曹芷馨自幼生活于中国南方，后因学业成绩优异而被某大学本科录取；大学毕业后，为进一步提升自己，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年又在中国人民大学历史系攻读硕士学位；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年硕士毕业后，很快即被北京大学出版社录用而成为编辑；对其而言，正值青春年华，故而对未来生活及职业期许具有美好憧憬，然而接下来发生的事情却令其始料未及，并从此彻底改变了其人生轨迹；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，因疫情封控期间新疆发生火灾事件，其与几位朋友在网上看到在北京市亮马河将有悼念新疆死难同胞的信息，遂与友人一起加入到当晚在亮马河桥上的悼念人群之中；但因中共当局针对各地的悼念活动以及由此发展起来的白纸抗议行动，纷纷采取严打逼迫的手段，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其及朋友等多人均被当地派出所警方传唤带走；后因都是年轻人，且都没有做出格的举动，故而在被传唤笔录和警方批评教育的<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时之后，又都无罪释放；然而同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，警方又将曹芷馨<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位好友在毫无征兆的情况下秘密刑拘，并且当时在抓捕令上签字时发现罪名栏目都是空白，警方也拒透所有被抓当事人的罪名、关押地点及时间，遂其深感不安，故专门制作了一段小视频，预备其不测后委托朋友发于网上，以求更多社会各界及国际组织的关注和声援；后，曹芷馨也很快被北京市朝阳区警方秘密抓捕、刑拘，罪名暂时不清。曹芷馨被羁押于北京市朝阳区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日获悉已取保获释。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: right 415.3pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_19.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_19.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: right 415.3pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_20.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_20.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">22</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李元婧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代出生，籍贯不详，北京某跨国会计事务所会计师，网络活跃人士，电报群群主，北京白纸运动参与者，中国在押政治犯。自研究生毕业后，即选择留在北京生活，并在北京市一跨国会计事务所当会计师；业余时间，因热爱交友而特意组建一电报群，让兴趣相投网友互通信息，发布、谈论及分享海内外信息、观念与看法，故而在朋友圈中拥有极好声誉；但又因该电报群里有不少海外媒体网友，其言论、信息时有对中共当局不利的信息，因而群内信息常被当局网警想尽办法予以突破和监控；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因新疆乌鲁木齐一栋大楼突发火灾，但政府当时的过度防疫措施而致火灾未能及时扑灭和救助，最终导致数十人死亡；消息一经传出，世界各地华人群体，尤其是海外留学生群体及中国大陆各地民众纷纷为死难者举行悼念和抗议活动；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其及多名群友与因在网上看到当晚在北京市朝阳区亮马河将有为新疆死难同胞悼念的活动信息，遂与曹芷馨、翟登蕊等数名好友带着蜡烛、鲜花以及写了诗句的便签与白纸，一起到亮马河桥上参与了悼念活动；孰料两天之后，其等十数名青年人尽都被当地派出所警方带走传唤；后因其等在悼念活动中并未有出格举动，因而一天之后尽被警方无罪释放；然而<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其又被北京市朝阳区警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”秘密刑拘，另有<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人亦在同天和之后几天内纷纷被朝阳区警方以同罪由二次刑拘，自此全都失联；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日获悉，其与同是白纸抗议者的群友李思琪、曹芷馨、翟登蕊等共计<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被北京市朝阳区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕。被羁押于北京市朝阳区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日获悉已取保获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_59.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_59.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_20.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_20.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">23</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、翟登蕊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，微信名阿拉登，甘肃白银人，女权活动组织者，曾经组织一个女权群，最近被解散。翟登蕊本科是社工，因热爱文学，又读北外文学研究生，是北外英美文学专业研究生毕业，曾在学而思工作过，疫情刚起来的时候，曾组织阅读费兰特著名的小说《我的天才女友》。翟登蕊是于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日遭北京警方抓捕，据悉她可能已被以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪批捕。翟登蕊生活里理性而温和，她的勇气令人感动，身材不太高，脾气温和。她关注性别权利，喜欢戏剧和教育<span lang="EN-US">,</span>可爱又热情，经常去养老院和公益机构做志愿工作，被抓捕前还在帮孩子们做英语演讲的培训。她母亲是抗疫一线医生，想不到自己善良热情的独生女儿会失去自由，春节也未释放。姥姥已<span lang="EN-US">86</span>高龄，常年有病，很想念外孙女。被以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪批捕，被羁押于北京市朝阳区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日获悉已取保获释。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_22.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_22.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_20.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_20.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">24</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、李思琪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代出生，独立记者，自由媒体人，网络活跃人士，北京白纸运动参与者，中国在押政治犯。自李思琪英国留学回来，其即在北京逐渐成为一名年轻有为的记者和自由媒体人；因其平常交际圈中有很多外媒朋友，故而在其加入的电报群里会经常将这些外媒人士拉进群中聊天；但因该电报群早已被中共警方解密破译，故而其等群友聊天记录都被警方掌控，只是其等群体并未意识而已；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因新疆乌鲁木齐一栋大楼突发火灾，但政府当时的过度防疫措施导致火灾未能及时扑灭与救助，最终使得数十人死亡；消息一经传出，世界各地华人群体，尤其是海外留学生群体及中国大陆各地民众纷纷为死难者举行悼念和抗议活动；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其及多名群友与在网上看到当晚在北京市朝阳区亮马河将有为新疆死难同胞悼念的活动信息，遂与电报群中的好友曹芷馨、李元婧等数名好友一起带着蜡烛、鲜花以及写了诗句的便签与白纸，到亮马河桥上参与了悼念活动；熟料两天之后，其等十数名青年人尽都被当地派出所警方带走传唤；后因其等在悼念活动中并未有出格举动，故一天之后又都被无罪释放；然而<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，李思琪又被北京市朝阳区警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”秘密带走、刑拘，另有<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人亦在同期几天之内纷纷被朝阳区警方以同罪由刑拘，自此全都失联；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日获悉，其与同是白纸抗议者的群友曹芷馨、李元靖等共计<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被北京市朝阳区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕；据悉，其被二次拘捕，主要与参加了亮马桥白纸抗议运动，并在电报群里经常拉进外媒人士，分享海内外信息和观念等有关。被羁押于北京市朝阳区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日获悉已取保获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_58.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_58.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_20.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">25</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、侯金艺</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，郑州人，曾留学据悉侯金艺白纸运动时去过亮马桥，第二天被警方带走，后取保。大年初三<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日其被郑州当局传唤后强迫失踪。后取保获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">附录二：本月获悉上期名录中狱中遭迫害致死的<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人的名单及简历<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">滕淑丽、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王建、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、滕淑丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>出生。黑龙江鸡西市法轮功学员。鸡西市法轮功学员周克铭在发放法轮功资料时，被人诬告。鸡西市公安局鸡冠区公安分局国保、永昌派出所、铁西派出所采取跟踪、监控手段，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日抓捕了包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被非法关押在鸡西市看守所<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。包万明、周克铭、滕淑丽，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日遭鸡东法院以视频的方式开庭，近日得知，包万明被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、罚金十万元；滕淑丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元；周克铭被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。滕淑丽刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被非法判刑七年的鸡西市<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁法轮功学员滕淑丽，在黑龙江省女子监狱对她精神和身体的摧残中，被迫害致死。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/8/458584.html"><span style="color: windowtext;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/8/458584.html</span></a><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、王建：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1950</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日王建被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日王建家属突然接到冀东监狱电话，说王建死亡。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/8/458597.html"><span style="color:
